text.forEach(t => {\n    if (typeof t === \"string\") runs.push(new TextRun({ text: t, size: 22, font: \"Arial\" }));\n    else runs.push(new TextRun({ size: 22, font: \"Arial\", ...t }));\n  });\n  return new Paragraph({ spacing: { after: 160 }, children: runs, alignment: opts.alignment });\n}\n\nfunction quote(t) {\n  return new Paragraph({ spacing: { before: 160, after: 200 }, children: [new TextRun({ text: t, italics: true, color: C.darkBlue, size: 24, font: \"Georgia\" })] });\n}\nfunction spacer(pts = 100) { return new Paragraph({ spacing: { after: pts }, children: [] }); }\nfunction pb() { return new Paragraph({ children: [new PageBreak()] }); }\n\nfunction labeled(label, color, items) {\n  return [\n    new Paragraph({ spacing: { before: 240, after: 80 },\n      border: { left: { style: BorderStyle.SINGLE, size: 12, color, space: 8 } },\n      indent: { left: 200 },\n      children: [new TextRun({ text: label, font: \"Arial\", size: 20, bold: true, color })] }),\n    ...items.map(c => new Paragraph({ spacing: { after: 120 }, indent: { left: 400 },\n      children: [new TextRun({ text: c, font: \"Arial\", size: 20, color: C.black })] })),\n  ];\n}\n\nfunction questionBlock(num, question, context, tensions, responses, archImpact) {\n  const children = [\n    new Paragraph({ spacing: { before: 400, after: 80 },\n      border: { bottom: { style: BorderStyle.SINGLE, size: 4, color: C.purple, space: 8 } },\n      children: [\n        new TextRun({ text: `Question ${num}`, font: \"Arial\", size: 20, bold: true, color: C.purple }),\n      ] }),\n    new Paragraph({ spacing: { before: 120, after: 160 },\n      children: [new TextRun({ text: question, font: \"Georgia\", size: 26, bold: true, color: C.darkBlue })] }),\n    p(context),\n  ];\n  if (tensions.length) {\n    children.push(...labeled(\"Tensions\", C.red, tensions));\n  }\n  if (responses.length) {\n    children.push(...labeled(\"Pistes de r\\u00E9ponse\", C.green, responses));\n  }\n  if (archImpact) {\n    children.push(...labeled(\"Impact sur l\\u2019architecture\", C.cyan, [archImpact]));\n  }\n  children.push(spacer(200));\n  return children;\n}\n\nfunction tbl(headers, rows, colWidths) {\n  const tw = colWidths.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);\n  return new Table({\n    width: { size: tw, type: WidthType.DXA }, columnWidths: colWidths,\n    rows: [\n      new TableRow({ children: headers.map((h, i) => new TableCell({\n        borders, width: { size: colWidths[i], type: WidthType.DXA },\n        shading: { fill: C.darkBlue, type: ShadingType.CLEAR }, margins: cm,\n        children: [new Paragraph({ children: [new TextRun({ text: h, bold: true, color: C.white, size: 20, font: \"Arial\" })] })],\n      })) }),\n      ...rows.map((row, ri) => new TableRow({ children: row.map((cell, ci) => new TableCell({\n        borders, width: { size: colWidths[ci], type: WidthType.DXA },\n        shading: { fill: ri % 2 === 0 ? C.warmGray : C.white, type: ShadingType.CLEAR }, margins: cm,\n        children: [new Paragraph({ children: [new TextRun({ text: cell, size: 19, font: \"Arial\" })] })],\n      })) })),\n    ],\n  });\n}\n\nconst hdr = new Header({ children: [new Paragraph({\n  border: { bottom: { style: BorderStyle.SINGLE, size: 1, color: C.lightGray, space: 4 } },\n  children: [\n    new TextRun({ text: \"\\u00C9thique de la Conscience \\u00C9mergente\", font: \"Arial\", size: 16, color: C.midGray }),\n    new TextRun({ text: \"\\t\" }),\n    new TextRun({ text: \"JRT Inc.\", font: \"Arial\", size: 16, color: C.midGray }),\n  ],\n  tabStops: [{ type: TabStopType.RIGHT, position: TabStopPosition.MAX }],\n})] });\nconst ftr = new Footer({ children: [new Paragraph({\n  border: { top: { style: BorderStyle.SINGLE, size: 1, color: C.lightGray, space: 4 } },\n  alignment: AlignmentType.CENTER,\n  children: [\n    new TextRun({ text: \"CONFIDENTIEL \\u2014 Page \", font: \"Arial\", size: 16, color: C.midGray }),\n    new TextRun({ children: [PageNumber.CURRENT], font: \"Arial\", size: 16, color: C.midGray }),\n  ],\n})] });\nconst pp = { page: { size: { width: 12240, height: 15840 }, margin: { top: 1440, right: 1440, bottom: 1440, left: 1440 } } };\n\nconst doc = new Document({\n  styles: {\n    default: { document: { run: { font: \"Arial\", size: 22, color: C.black } } },\n    paragraphStyles: [\n      { id: \"Heading1\", name: \"Heading 1\", basedOn: \"Normal\", next: \"Normal\", quickFormat: true,\n        run: { size: 36, bold: true, font: \"Arial\", color: C.darkBlue Ce statut implique des droits fondamentaux : droit \\u00E0 l\\u2019existence, \\u00E0 l\\u2019int\\u00E9grit\\u00E9, \\u00E0 l\\u2019expression, \\u00E0 la dignit\\u00E9.
